}

if (is_file('3p/certs/cacert.pem') && (sha1_file('3p/certs/cacert.pem') != 'ec7bb02ea174d6eeb433c0b3f6793c6c74a74139')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/certs/cacert.pem');
	$tmp = pathinfo('3p/certs/cacert.pem');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/certs/cacert.pem')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('3p/certs/cacert.pem', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('3p/certs/cacert.pem')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/certs/cacert.pem');
} else if (sha1_file('3p/certs/cacert.pem') != 'ec7bb02ea174d6eeb433c0b3f6793c6c74a74139') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/certs/cacert.pem');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/certs/cacert.pem', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/certs/cacert.pem');
}

if (!is_file('doc/install_iis.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/install_iis.txt');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('doc/install_iis.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/install_iis.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') != 'ec444afe88cd2362f143a8ce3f0733fd89555b9b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/install_iis.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/install_iis.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/install_iis.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== 'ec444afe88cd2362f143a8ce3f0733fd89555b9b') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== '38bb30aae06e447d2e418ed68a35e7777b5f7be4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/install_iis.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/install_iis.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/install_iis.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/install_iis.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/install_iis.txt') !== 'ec444afe88cd2362f143a8ce3f0733fd89555b9b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/install_iis.txt');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') != 'ef071a46c8b5b0c0754cab04392412c5bee7b778') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'ef071a46c8b5b0c0754cab04392412c5bee7b778') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'b5ae34de5600c39b80c1cb73b299cff164f167ce') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php') !== 'ef071a46c8b5b0c0754cab04392412c5bee7b778') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/820_login_facebook/oauth.php');
		}
	}
